     01EF             (     downland.asm):00234         Drop0_CeilingWiggleTimer_0x1ef equ 0x01ef                            ; Each drop data is 13 bytes long.
                      (     downland.asm):00235                                                                              ; byte : description
                      (     downland.asm):00236                                                                              ; 0: state / ceiling wiggle countdown 
                      (     downland.asm):00237                                                                              ;     values:
                      (     downland.asm):00238                                                                              ;     0: disabled
                      (     downland.asm):00239                                                                              ;     1: initialized but not running
                      (     downland.asm):00240                                                                              ;        will be initialized next update
                      (     downland.asm):00241                                                                              ;     0xA8 - 0x80: wiggling
                      (     downland.asm):00242                                                                              ;     0x7F: falling
                      (     downland.asm):00243                                                                              ; 1-2: drop speed (0x200 falling, 
                      (     downland.asm):00244                                                                              ;                  toggles between 0x80 and
                      (     downland.asm):00245                                                                              ;                  0xff80 when jiggling to
                      (     downland.asm):00246                                                                              ;                  move up and down)
                      (     downland.asm):00247                                                                              ; 3-4: y position (pixel + subpixel)
                      (     downland.asm):00248                                                                              ; 5: x position (0 - 127)
                      (     downland.asm):00249                                                                              ; 6-7: location of sprite in ram
                      (     downland.asm):00250                                                                              ; 8-9: draw location in video page
                      (     downland.asm):00251                                                                              ; 10-11 (a-b): previous frame draw location in video page
                      (     downland.asm):00252                                                                              ; 12 (c): the collision mask of the bottom of the drop.
                      (     downland.asm):00253                                                                              ;         the mask is different depending on which frame
                      (     downland.asm):00254                                                                              ;         of the drop sprite it uses.
                      (     downland.asm):00255                                                                              ; 
     01F0             (     downland.asm):00256         Drop0_SpeedY_01f0 equ 0x01f0                                         
     01F2             (     downland.asm):00257         Drop0_Y_0x1f2 equ 0x01f2

                      (     downland.asm):01108         ;The "mysterious sprites" located between the player and
                      (     downland.asm):01109         ;ball sprites in rom data are masks used to extract five
                      (     downland.asm):01110         ;lines across the player sprite on the screen. The extracted
                      (     downland.asm):01111         ;lines are then compared to a clean version of the player

                      (     downland.asm):01113         ;the extracted pixels and the clean version triggers a

                      (     downland.asm):01115         ;moving objects.

D852 A624             (     downland.asm):05712                 LDA        0x4,Y                                             
D854 E626             (     downland.asm):05713                 LDB        0x6,Y                                             
                      (     downland.asm):05714         ;**************************************************************
                      (     downland.asm):05715         ;* Generates a memory location in a video page for            *
                      (     downland.asm):05716         ;* the given X and Y.                                         *
                      (     downland.asm):05717         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05718         ;* A register holds the Y position (0 - 191)                  *
                      (     downland.asm):05719         ;* B register holds the X position (0 - 127)                  *
                      (     downland.asm):05720         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05721         ;* Note that X works in half resolution, not 256              *
                      (     downland.asm):05722         ;* pixels like the current screen mode. The function          *
                      (     downland.asm):05723         ;* scales X up so that it maps to the screen res.             *
                      (     downland.asm):05724         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05725         ;* To find the correct byte along the X axis, it first        *
                      (     downland.asm):05726         ;* doubles X to map its position to 256 pixels. Then it       *
                      (     downland.asm):05727         ;* divides by 8 (bits) to find the corresponding byte in      *
                      (     downland.asm):05728         ;* video memory.                                              *
                      (     downland.asm):05729         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05730         ;* Formula:                                                   *
                      (     downland.asm):05731         ;* offset = (Y * screen_width_in_bytes) + (X * 2 / 8)         *
                      (     downland.asm):05732         ;* final pos = offset + video_memory_location                 *
                      (     downland.asm):05733         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05734         ;* example:                                                   *
                      (     downland.asm):05735         ;* (0x24 * 0x20) + (0x4f * 2 / 8) + 0x400 = 0x893 (893.C)     *
                      (     downland.asm):05736         ;*                                                            *
                      (     downland.asm):05737         ;* background draw origin point: Y:0x10, X:0xF                *
                      (     downland.asm):05738         ;* (0x10 * 0x20) + (0xf * 2 / 8) + 0x400 = 0x603 (603.C)      *
                      (     downland.asm):05739         ;**************************************************************
                      (     downland.asm):05740         ;undefined __stdcall ComputeScreenLocationFromAAndB(void)
                      (     downland.asm):05741         ;undefined         A:1            <RETURN>
                      (     downland.asm):05742
